20/08/bilibili_meitu_15.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn30@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-28-630_6577da5537345d4d.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/006JTzz0ly1fyudodnzpqj30nj0d8nlc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn2@2020_1/2020/08/31/17-24-33-875_85fa63ab6beb467a.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fortnite-4129124_1920-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn19@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-33-189_a6c12df45909ad26.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/IMG_3558.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn50@2020_1/2020/08/31/17-24-30-102_7465f716cb20ca13.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/200603.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn39@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-27-582_d4d78b9c19295844.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/IMG_3559.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn83@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-25-975_f14c8e16e3087d22.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/0-5.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn42@2020_2/2020/08/31/17-24-25-999_c017fc8f02fb9c58.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/IMG_3561.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn80@2020_6/2020/08/31/17-24-31-864_4da36472f858130d.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/mode_pic5.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn29@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-30-384_6fc12a4dde19cb65.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598894642703},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","title":"噢，上帝啊！翻译腔到底该不该死？","link":"https://www.ifanr.com/?p=1361161&utm_source=rss&utm_medium=rss&utm_campaign=","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361378\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/969.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"650\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/969.png 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/969-360x195.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/969-768x416.png 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/969-1024x555.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p>\n<p>为了保证更沉浸式的阅读体验，先来看看《泰坦尼克号》这段对话：</p>\n<blockquote><p>喔我的天哪，杰克，你快上来，别泡在海里了。<br />\n噢，真该死，柔丝，这块该死的木头承受不了两个人的重量，我上去一定会翻的。<br />\n天哪，亲爱的，杰克，我爱你。<br />\n噢！我的柔丝，我也爱你。</p></blockquote>\n<p>是不是脑袋里已经回响起被翻译腔支配的旋律了。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361245\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/111-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1017\" height=\"683\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/111-1.jpg 706w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/111-1-360x242.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1017px) 100vw, 1017px\" /></p>\n<p>当年，人人嗑着瓜子守在 CCTV6 观看时，也并未觉得这些译制片不妥。只是现在再回头，恐怕都会因为那刻意的翻译腔出戏。</p>\n<p>更让人印象深刻的，还有这些翻译腔台词：</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361249\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG201.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"3072\" height=\"996\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG201.jpeg 3072w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG201-360x117.jpeg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG201-768x249.jpeg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG201-1024x332.jpeg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 3072px) 100vw, 3072px\" /></p>\n<p>夸张的鼻音在回响，字字发音圆润饱满；魔性的语调在盘旋，句句收尾颤音绕梁。</p>\n<p>不过历史悠久的翻译腔恐怕也没有想到，自己还能在互联网时代重回青春。</p>\n<h3>一场大型翻译腔模仿秀</h3>\n<p>什么是翻译腔？</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:%E7%BF%BB%E8%AF%91%E8%85%94\">正经来说，</a>翻译腔就是翻译外国文化作品时，翻译者有意或无意地直译某些词汇，形成不符合汉语表达习惯的一种独特腔调。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://baijiahao.baidu.com/s?id=1637205349723423026&#38;wfr=spider&#38;for=pc\">这些腔调最早来自于</a> 1948 年 1 月 8 日，上海大戏院公映由 20 多个华侨译配的意大利影片《一舞难忘》，同年 9 月，「东北电影制片厂」成立翻版组，正式开创了我国电影译制事业的先河。</p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361262\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/898-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1047\" height=\"739\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/898-3.png 737w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/898-3-360x254.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1047px) 100vw, 1047px\" /></p>\n<p>▲ 1949 年 5 月，《普通一兵》的译制标志着中国第一部真正意义上的译制片出现。</p>\n</div>\n<p>八九十年代开始，越来越多国外影视文化作品开始引进。为了让外国电影看起来更像外国电影，外国书籍看起来更像外国书籍，既有洋味儿，又有洋范儿，翻译腔就来了。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361248\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/timg.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"900\" height=\"500\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/timg.gif 900w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/timg-360x200.gif 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/timg-768x427.gif 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 900px) 100vw, 900px\" /></p>\n<p>这些欧式翻译腔大致遵循了以下五大要素：</p>\n<ul>\n<li>无论见到谁，称呼都要听起来和对方很熟，如老伙计，好家伙；</li>\n<li>没事就「我打赌」「我保证」，看起来信心十足，激情澎湃；</li>\n<li>喜欢踢屁股、骂土拨鼠、开隔壁邻居玩笑；</li>\n<li>最后，请让上帝和圣母玛利亚的光环时刻照耀。</li>\n</ul>\n<p>学会这几招，你就能开始你的模仿秀了。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361265\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG203.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1074\" height=\"320\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG203.jpeg 1074w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG203-360x107.jpeg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG203-768x229.jpeg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG203-1024x305.jpeg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1074px) 100vw, 1074px\" /></p>\n<p>随着欧式翻译腔被挖坟，日式翻译腔也紧随其后被摆上了台面。</p>\n<p>它比起欧式翻译腔低调柔和了许多，第一次看到，让人联想到富士山上那明亮而洁白的初雪：</p>\n<blockquote><p>米娜桑是怀着对天下美好的期盼来的吧，真是让人无法拒绝呢。</p></blockquote>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361254 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1941598490934_.pic_.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"406\" height=\"166\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1941598490934_.pic_.jpg 718w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1941598490934_.pic_-360x147.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 406px) 100vw, 406px\" /></p>\n<p>宿命、羁绊等热血词汇高频出现，每个人都是自己的救世主：</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p class=\"p1\">为什么！为什么让我看到这个！明明<span class=\"s1\">&#8230;&#8230;</span>明明我不想看到的啊<span class=\"s1\">&#8230;&#8230;</span>可恶！到此为止了么。玄德君的用心良苦什么的，我应该早点察觉才对啊混蛋！</p>\n<p>尽管宿命是像樱花般微弱而容易消逝，但也想让这个世界听到我们的声音啊，怀着这种卑微而甜蜜的心情的我，玄德君一定会懂得吧！</p>\n<p class=\"p1\">请务必让我获得最后的优胜吧，拜托了！</p>\n</blockquote>\n<p>听起来也很有礼貌，呐、呢、啊等语气助词频繁被使用，每句话都仿佛在挣扎和纠结中艰难吐露。</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361268 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-3369811f7c7727da4fc634a11b29c5da_720w.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"354\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-3369811f7c7727da4fc634a11b29c5da_720w.jpg 500w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-3369811f7c7727da4fc634a11b29c5da_720w-360x575.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 354px) 100vw, 354px\" /></p>\n<p>还有一种迷之羞耻感在空气中发酵，甚至隐隐透露出一丝「绿茶」的味道：</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361274 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/78-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"365\" height=\"60\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/78-1.png 572w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/78-1-360x59.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 365px) 100vw, 365px\" /></p>\n<p>比起日式翻译腔，韩式翻译腔听起来就很大大咧咧了：</p>\n<blockquote>\n<ul>\n<li>女：呀！臭小子！</li>\n<li>男：你这女人是疯了吗？！真是&#8230;&#8230;</li>\n<li>女：呀！要不要交往试试？</li>\n<li>男：阿西&#8230;&#8230; 你死定了！</li>\n</ul>\n</blockquote>\n<p>德式翻译腔则显得格外严谨，一眼望去，高深莫测：</p>\n<blockquote><p>我以上的表达的一切内容及其形式违背了诸位的不成熟的意愿，以至于使得诸位对我产生了本不应该产生的意见 —— 即我得罪了诸位。</p></blockquote>\n<p>眼看着国外的翻译腔兴风作浪，网民们自然也不会放过我们博大精深的汉语言。</p>\n<p>「文言文腔」成了「中国腔」的代表，网友们挖出了它含蓄而婉转的特性，前面铺垫一大段话，都是为了结尾道出一个出乎意料的人生哲理，好让听闻之人醍醐灌顶：</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361269 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-9ff5a040590c28b97255f8ff2434fdc9_720w.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"367\" height=\"362\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-9ff5a040590c28b97255f8ff2434fdc9_720w.jpg 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-9ff5a040590c28b97255f8ff2434fdc9_720w-360x355.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 367px) 100vw, 367px\" /></p>\n<p>结构之复杂，言辞之丰满，令人想起小学在老师面前背不出课文的恐惧。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361311\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"779\" height=\"248\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123.png 682w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123-360x115.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 779px) 100vw, 779px\" /></p>\n<p>同时，更「细分」的领域也开始发展，网民们从国外放眼国内，模仿发嗲功力深厚的台湾腔，也模仿句句洒脱的「香港 TVB 腔」：</p>\n<blockquote><p>阿 sir，做人呐，最重要的就是开心。</p></blockquote>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361273\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/667.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1040\" height=\"587\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/667.jpeg 622w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/667-360x203.jpeg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1040px) 100vw, 1040px\" /></p>\n<p>随着人们的文化水平变高，早期的译制片时代由盛转衰，原声配字幕的形式逐渐普及。</p>\n<p>翻译腔也不再特指翻译外语的腔调，不再是转述一个旧时代的故事，而是变成了一种新的娱乐方式。</p>\n<p>这种娱乐方式就像一场模仿秀，人人都能轻松参与，快速制造交流对话中的快乐源泉。</p>\n<p>当国家的分类也满足不了网友喷发的创作欲时，「翻译腔」就不再受地点限制，开始新一轮「变体」。</p>\n<h3>万物皆可「翻译腔」</h3>\n<p>一直以来，翻译都是桥梁般的存在。</p>\n<p>当「翻译」成为当代互联网世界沟通会晤之桥时，任何一种有着自我风格的语言，都可以转变成一种独特的「腔体」。</p>\n<p>某一部剧、一部电影、一种现象火起来时，大家热议的台词，很快就会被「翻译」到日常对话中来。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.douban.com/group/689597/?ref=sidebar\">豆瓣小组「翻译腔」</a>，成了「腔浪」们的最全集合处。</p>\n<p>B 站的「后浪」视频掀起舆论浪潮时，网民们都开始模仿演讲者何冰那气宇轩昂、心系天下的「后浪腔」：</p>\n<blockquote><p>奔涌吧！腔浪们！</p></blockquote>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361259\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1881598490758_.pic_.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1078\" height=\"482\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1881598490758_.pic_.jpg 664w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1881598490758_.pic_-360x161.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1078px) 100vw, 1078px\" /></p>\n<p>还有一种「翻译腔」盛行在微博上，就是「饭圈控评腔」。</p>\n<p>这里的每一句语调都绽放出爱与崇拜的烟花，这里每个人的声音都热闹得仿佛大年初一的礼炮。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361253\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1931598490933_.pic_hd.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2055\" height=\"1376\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1931598490933_.pic_hd.jpg 2055w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1931598490933_.pic_hd-360x241.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1931598490933_.pic_hd-768x514.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1931598490933_.pic_hd-1024x686.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2055px) 100vw, 2055px\" /></p>\n<p>一些在人们心中留下不可磨灭的华彩与阴影的影视剧，也会常年被拿出来津津乐道。</p>\n<p>当闺蜜群里的姐妹开始吵吵嚷嚷时，撕逼圣典「小时代腔」来了：</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361381 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG212.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"345\" height=\"613\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG212.jpeg 1242w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG212-360x640.jpeg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG212-768x1365.jpeg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG212-576x1024.jpeg 576w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 345px) 100vw, 345px\" /></p>\n<p>当同事开始假装尔虞我诈时，狠话手册「甄嬛腔」来了：</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361284 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG209-1.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"340\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG209-1.jpeg 1228w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG209-1-360x317.jpeg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG209-1-768x677.jpeg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG209-1-1024x902.jpeg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 340px) 100vw, 340px\" /></p>\n<p>当语言不足以表达内心的万千愤慨时，「祖安腔」都来了：</p>\n<blockquote><p>**********，***，******，*******。******，****！</p></blockquote>\n<p>这似乎成了人们走在互联网前线必备的一种技能。</p>\n<p>如果哪天你听不懂这些「翻译腔」里的梗，就像提前步入了更年期。</p>\n<p>所以与此同时，另一波「反前线」的「翻译腔体」也开始出现，他们创造出了「过时网络用语腔」。</p>\n<p>打开「过时网络用语腔」，遍地的 QQ 爱，是真是假没人猜，问今年你几岁，有过几次 one night，吓得我发呆，这是什么 e 时代。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361258\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1891598490804_.pic_.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1047\" height=\"573\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1891598490804_.pic_.jpg 663w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1891598490804_.pic_-360x197.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1047px) 100vw, 1047px\" /></p>\n<p>谈到复古怀旧风，「中老年朋友圈腔」自然也少不了。</p>\n<p>祝福、吉祥、感恩，是三大叔八大姨们朋友圈里的关键词：</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361257\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1901598490837_.pic_.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1003\" height=\"549\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1901598490837_.pic_.jpg 663w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1901598490837_.pic_-360x197.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1003px) 100vw, 1003px\" /></p>\n<p>随着越来越多人口耳相传，翻译腔从基础形态，到进化形态，再变成放养生态。</p>\n<p>它不仅仅是一种娱乐方式，而是成为了一种互联网文化符号。</p>\n<p>当人们制造网络狂欢时，传统语言与网络新生词也在碰撞中混合交融，「翻译」的过程，也是语言被洞察、传播、改变的过程。</p>\n<h3>翻译腔到底是不是一件好事？</h3>\n<p>回过头来看，从具有浓厚时代印记的翻译腔，到充满现代娱乐色彩的「翻译腔」，它们的出现到底是不是一件好事？</p>\n<p>早期来看，出现在译制片里的语调，其实是为了保持影视画面和声音的同步，才会在语速、语调等地方进行调整，这背后其实需要<a href=\"https://www.douban.com/note/687410470/\">翻译人员付出很大努力</a>。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361320\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/99999-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1029\" height=\"561\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/99999-1.png 818w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/99999-1-360x196.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/99999-1-768x419.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1029px) 100vw, 1029px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲图片来自：《美丽人生》</p>\n</div>\n<p>他们要数口型、数节奏，再翻译、对口型，这使得原本简短的中文要为配合画面来加减台词，配音演员也要用夸张的腔调来模仿演员的表演风格，以符合那时人们对遥远异邦的想象。</p>\n<p>当时很多人文化水平不高，识字率低，重新配音能让更多人看懂外国的优秀电影。</p>\n<p>虽然现在译制片的腔调已渐渐淡出市场，但当时的翻译腔，是有助于电影事业发展壮大的。</p>\n<p>而现在的影视作品尤其是书籍作品中，翻译腔一直都存在着巨大的争议。</p>\n<p>这争议被分为两派，一是「异化」组，另一个是「归化」组。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361302\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-91442638ae1925072e3474f6d6d111a2_720w.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1020\" height=\"573\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-91442638ae1925072e3474f6d6d111a2_720w.jpg 600w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-91442638ae1925072e3474f6d6d111a2_720w-360x202.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1020px) 100vw, 1020px\" /></p>\n<p>前者认为翻译腔应该维持原语言的原汁原味，保留原语言的陌生感，这样能让读者多了解、感知、传播文本背后的另一个文明；后者认为翻译腔应该让原语言本土化，淡化原语言的陌生感，不能被外界侵袭改造本土文化。</p>\n<p>诺贝尔文学奖得主 Seamus·Heaney 也曾<a href=\"https://baijiahao.baidu.com/s?id=1637205349723423026&#38;wfr=spider&#38;for=pc\">提出类似「异化」的观点</a>：</p>\n<blockquote><p>译者应适当抛弃语言的一般表达方式，将目的语的表达世界变得陌生，更新读者对语言新鲜感的接受能力，使原作中的差异能够传达出来，以促进不同民族间相互理解和交流。</p></blockquote>\n<p>拿日本的文学作品来说，我们日常语气说的一句话「现实里是不会有那种怦然心动的感觉的」，变成日本轻小说里，可能就成了「怦然心动什么的，那种东西现实里才不会有呢！」</p>\n<p>其中的翻译腔，不仅看得出日本独特的语言结构，委婉客气的语言风格，还有日本人常在言语间留有余地的个性。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361321\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/789-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1045\" height=\"585\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/789-1.png 652w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/789-1-360x202.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1045px) 100vw, 1045px\" /></p>\n<p>更多人担忧和抗拒的是，「异化」的翻译读起来诘屈聱牙，汉语结构和韵律美感消失殆尽。</p>\n<p>这也是很多人支持翻译「归化」的原因。</p>\n<p>毕竟将外文转变成大家习以为常的本土化语言，确实会更熟悉、舒服、易理解。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361299\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-6f8cf67ea9a43c6c54e12fd7e90833a9_720w.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1157\" height=\"651\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-6f8cf67ea9a43c6c54e12fd7e90833a9_720w.jpg 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2-6f8cf67ea9a43c6c54e12fd7e90833a9_720w-360x203.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1157px) 100vw, 1157px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲「归化」的翻译腔</p>\n</div>\n<p>不过要指出的是，有些很拗口和难懂的翻译腔，其实是译者因自身能力不足或图快速省事，就直接简单粗暴地将外文翻译成对应的中文，不加任何润色和修饰。</p>\n<p><strong>这最后呈现的根本就不是翻译腔，而是翻错腔。</strong></p>\n<p>毕竟转换两种语言，是要花很多时间的。高质量的翻译其实就等于是再创作，译者本身就得具备极高的写作水准。</p>\n<p>翻译不仅首先要保证内容准确、语法结构顺畅，还要还原历史社会环境、语言背后的情感典故、揣摩作者所思所想、将文章得体优雅呈现，才能达到翻译的「信达雅」。</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1361312\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123456.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1079\" height=\"445\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123456.png 822w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123456-360x148.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/123456-768x317.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1079px) 100vw, 1079px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ <a href=\"https://www.douban.com/note/720692656/\">授衣翻译的《骡子》台词</a></p>\n</div>\n<p>所以<strong>翻译腔本身不应该是一个贬义词</strong>。正如「看理想」签约作者李如一所说：</p>\n<blockquote><p>好的翻译腔好，坏的翻译腔坏。</p></blockquote>\n<p>关于保护汉语言一说，尽管有其道理，但事实上，<strong>我们已经处于一个语言不断变化的时代</strong>。</p>\n<p>翻译腔已经完全融入我们的日常生活之中，从文言文到五四时期的白话文，从新闻联播到网络对话，各类变体的「翻译腔」，无论是语法和文字上，都已经顺势日益改变，也丰富了汉语的词汇和句式。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.zhihu.com/question/33949674?from=profile_question_card\">王小波认为，</a>现代汉语是翻译家们塑造的。</p>\n<p>当人人都开始参与「语言的翻译」时，不管以何种形式，语言体系都在更加快速更迭之中。</p>\n<p>「翻译腔」贯穿在语言进化的路上，也和语言一样，不只是工具，而是承载着文化的发展和演变。</p>\n<p>每个人看剧或读书时，感受到的翻译腔是「原文再现」还是「再创造」，心中都有自己度量的尺子。</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-1361318 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG211.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"709\" height=\"518\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG211.jpeg 674w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG211-360x263.jpeg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 709px) 100vw, 709px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲冯唐和郑振铎分别翻译泰戈尔的《飞鸟集》. 图片来自：知乎账号-愿风裁尘</p>\n</div>\n<p>每个译者也有自己内心的尺子。正如日语翻译学者施小炜所说：</p>\n<blockquote><p>原作只有一个，却只要有一百个译者，便会有一百种译文。只要是立足于对原著正确理解基础之上的译文，便自有其存在的理由。</p></blockquote>\n<p>那么，就尊重每一种艺术呈现形式吧。</p>\n<p>一起来留下人类早期驯服翻译腔的珍贵影像吧。</p>\n<p>#欢迎关注爱范儿官方微信公众号：爱范儿（微信号：ifanr），更多精彩内容第一时间为您奉上。</p><p>\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com\">爱范儿</a> |\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1361161\">原文链接</a> ·\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1361161#comments\">查看评论</a> ·\n<a +0000","feedId":147,"bgimg":"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5d48755d100a24735441cf6b.jpeg","linkMd5":"cf21a1982c74e2aae19fcda9b2ea1eef","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn68@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-03-213_246f70666213ba72.webp","destWidth":1100,"destHeight":825,"sourceBytes":104283,"destBytes":91046,"author":"方嘉文","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5d48755d100a24735441cf6b.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn68@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-03-213_246f70666213ba72.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/jinri.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn87@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-26-130_9126976ba4a712d7.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/iPad-and-watch-soon-2.jpg":null,"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/apple_eec_watches_ipads.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn47@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-30-846_573b8a5c308cfd52.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/e007a6d439ab4fa598fd0b5e527e5c29.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn24@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-32-223_57f01ff71aa7114f.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/1597039501_949383.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn99@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-27-409_1ef3d88b7ec9431c.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/keji.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn71@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-30-871_66327f2ce05b8d5a.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled_2.0.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn14@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-30-174_8e99ed32b3d287dd.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/v2_6b113b4793f346a789ad00080b752e76_img_jpg.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn29@2020_6/2020/08/31/17-24-29-939_ecdab5711e8da281.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/6373405109638959418276113-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn65@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-29-025_fc945135a37761cf.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/dagongs.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn67@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-34-347_8636e83ec7b8885f.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fortnite_apple_featured.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn72@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-34-454_7d00fb7eb2095010.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3e78baa60932dd0.jpg":null,"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/lei.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn5@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-29-362_3f4332e5948db371.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bil.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn15@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-28-241_76dd116e92131759.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/citylife.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn16@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-26-218_441071b14a1b8e80.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/rolls-royce-pentagram-branding-design_dezeen_2364_col_9.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn76@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-27-237_2489b706539b8a70.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/rolls-royce-pentagram-branding-design_dezeen_2364_col_21.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn60@2020_2/2020/08/31/17-24-30-961_57caefcdb35a5cd8.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/222-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn6@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-28-086_eb75e784a4941b05.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG509.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn55@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-28-100_f0e00bd3076f82d2.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/shutterstock_editorial_8222802c.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn62@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-31-326_210411f94b9eb51c.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/wangyo.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn41@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-28-645_dd995d4740e9fa17.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/thur.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn7@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-33-305_6e2310e0a7eeeeb0.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/RISE_WIN_007re.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn83@2020_1/2020/08/31/17-24-33-114_ee63153d769e94c8.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/re.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn90@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-29-190_cfca56f4b90bb78d.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/RISE_WIN_019.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn16@2020_6/2020/08/31/17-24-27-713_2c06432e16599531.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598894642715},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","title":"卖「孤寡」年入 30 万，「线上慰问」服务居然这么多花样？","link":"https://www.ifanr.com/?p=1360969&utm_source=rss&utm_medium=rss&utm_campaign=","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361034\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1436\" height=\"816\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14.png 1436w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14-360x205.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14-768x436.png 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14-1024x582.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1436px) 100vw, 1436px\" /></p> \n<p>昨天，你被「孤寡」了吗？</p> \n<p>七夕节当天，不少人都收到了损友发来的「线上慰问」，根据淘宝官方给出的数据，这个看上去不正经的「七夕青蛙」，七夕前一天竟然有 36 万人搜索过。</p> \n<p>「孤寡」服务内容说起来很简单，一个悲伤蛙头像的微信号或者 QQ 号加完好友说明来意，立即发送一长串悲伤蛙表情和「孤寡」两个字的信息。</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361020\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1299\" height=\"1151\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4.png 1299w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4-360x319.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4-768x680.png 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4-1024x907.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1299px) 100vw, 1299px\" /></p> \n<p>一个在中国传统文化语境中并不吉利的词汇，却在一个中国传统文化节日中受到了大多数人喜爱，不少人把收到「孤寡线上慰问」视为有人关心自己的象征，分享到社交渠道进一步传播了「孤寡」这个概念。</p> \n<p>除了「孤寡」，你还能给朋友点些什么「线上慰问」服务？</p> \n<h3><strong>线上慰问服务有哪些？</strong></h3> \n<p>「线上特殊慰问」服务一直存在，打开淘宝，你会发现可购买的服务超出你的想象，服务价格从几元到几十元不等，大多数都在 20 元以内。</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361024\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"2523\" height=\"1812\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1.png 2523w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1-360x259.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1-768x552.png 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1-1024x735.png 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2523px) 100vw, 2523px\" /></p> \n<p>比较常见的有线上早午晚安服务，一般服务方会把文字或语音发到买家指定的账号上。一位淘宝店家告诉爱范儿：「我们店里卖的晚安比较多，大多数是男顾客买了，让我们发给他的女朋友或者暗恋对象。」</p> \n<p>特殊一点的线上慰问服务有表白、分手、复合、道歉、夸人、叫醒起床、监督完成作业等，「道歉的销量比较少，叫醒起床和监督完成作业还挺多的，有很多是自己买给自己的。」淘宝数据显示，七夕前一周，约 100 万人在淘宝上「求复合」，20 万人定制表白短信。</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361041\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua20.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"818\" height=\"522\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua20.png 818w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua20-360x230.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua20-768x490.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 818px) 100vw, 818px\" /></p> \n<p>店铺卖家告诉我们，线上慰问很早之前就有人开始做，「iPhone 4 流行那会儿就开始了吧，之前的渠道有短信、飞信、QQ，现在微信比较多」，行业已经比较成熟，「之前不是流行夸夸群吗，其实一开始也是收费夸奖服务，后来变成大家进群互相夸奖。」</p> \n<blockquote>\n <p>「让我最难忘的是一个买家给自己去世的老婆买晚安，每天一条，买了 3 年多，突然有一天我们发送（线上慰问服务）的手机号回短信，说号码换了主人，我们把情况告诉买家，买家第二天就说不发了，说要从过去走出来。」</p>\n</blockquote> \n<h3><strong>量身定做，自导自演</strong></h3> \n<p>为了满足饭圈群体的需求，店家还推出了线上恋人服务，店家会把微信账号头像换成买家指定的明星，用该明星的说话方式和粉丝互动，颇有几分养成类游戏的感觉。</p> \n<blockquote>\n <p>「这种（线上恋人）就比较贵了，因为是量身定做的，需要有剧情。我们的店铺小哥说自己做这个都快要做到精分了，一会是朱一龙，一会儿是易烊千玺。」</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361038\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1388\" height=\"684\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19.jpg 1388w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19-360x177.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19-768x378.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19-1024x505.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1388px) 100vw, 1388px\" /></p> \n<p>卖家说，除了定制线上恋人，买家想要什么服务，就可以有什么服务，「都是线上的，大家图个开心，也不会有人当真」。卖家表示他曾收到过一个线上骂人服务的需求，「第一时间拒绝了，这样做不好。」</p> \n<p>当然，卖家说这行也不是看上去那么简单，被买家挑剔服务质量，还有被收信方拒绝的也不少。</p> \n<p>「有些人会觉得这种服务有点奇怪，会要求我们别发了。」卖家表示只要对方有一次明确的拒绝，他们就会立即道歉并终止服务，「绝对不会透露买家的信息，这是（行业）规范。」</p> \n<p>也有不少人表示抵触「孤寡」这个词，感觉社会对单身人士存在满满的恶意，有一种被催婚的感觉，未经本人允许就「孤寡孤寡」更是一种社交「越界」，「单身（这个状态）不应该在七夕或者情人节被用来戏谑，自嘲可以，但是不要拿来嘲笑别人。」</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361057\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1038\" height=\"568\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23.jpg 1038w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23-360x197.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23-768x420.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23-1024x560.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1038px) 100vw, 1038px\" /></p> \n<div class=\"editor-image-source\"> \n <p>▲ 抵制「孤寡」的网友制作了「不孤鸟」表情包回击</p> \n</div> \n<p>总体来说，享受服务的人还是大多数。说起收入，爱范儿采访的两个商家给出了不同的结果，一个商家只通过淘宝店销售，年入大约几万元，另一个商家不仅有淘宝店，还有一家位于广州市长洲岛上的茶吧：「来的客人我都加了微信，近几年积累下来很多个账号加满了，有时候会把别人买的晚安发在朋友圈，后来通过微信买的人就多了，去年晚安告白求复合求原谅之类的加起来收入 30 多万。」</p> \n<h3><strong>给自己买了一份告白服务，爱了爱了</strong></h3> \n<p>为了亲身体验线上慰问服务，我花了 15 元购买了一份小哥哥在线告白服务。</p> \n<p>沟通好告白文案后，卖家让我通过一个微信账号的好友申请，说「他会向你告白。」</p> \n<p>不到 2 分钟，一个正在比心的名叫「吴彦祖」的「易烊千玺」加我了。</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361036\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua16.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"842\" height=\"476\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua16.png 842w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua16-360x204.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua16-768x434.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 842px) 100vw, 842px\" /></p> \n<p>我想翻看「吴彦祖」的朋友圈，发现他根本就没有朋友圈，有点小失望。</p> \n<p>但是当我听到「吴彦祖」的表白时，整个人都酥了，鸡皮疙瘩掉了一地，汗毛竖立起来变得格外敏感，觉得这 15 元花得太值了。</p> \n<p>分享给大家，一起欣赏吧，可以自行脑补一个播音主持版的易烊千玺在向自己告白。</p> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361050\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua22.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"827\" height=\"820\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua22.jpg 827w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua22-360x357.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua22-768x761.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 827px) 100vw, 827px\" /></p> \n<p>服务专业，声音好听，这是我对本次服务的总体评价，身为一个单身直男竟然有点心动的感觉，体验到了久违的温暖，爱了爱了。</p> \n<h3><strong>害羞和孤独是「线上慰问」的动力</strong></h3> \n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1361029\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1686\" height=\"1812\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10.png 1686w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10-360x387.png 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10-768x825.png 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10-953x1024.png 953w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1686px) 100vw, 1686px\" /></p> \n<p>不难发现，不少线上慰问服务完全可以由买家自己去做。</p> \n<p>比如男性对女性表白，比如七夕这次的「孤寡」慰问，还有每天的晚安等等，为什么有人宁愿花钱也要让人代劳？</p> \n<p>这和我们传统文化和现代社会结构有关。</p> \n<p>在中国的社交场景中，直来直去会被人觉得冒昧，很多时候我们觉得绕几个圈，把信息委婉地传递给对方才是恰到好处的表达方式。</p> \n<p>例如，外国人动不动就说 I love you，中国人会说「愿我如星君如月，夜夜流光相皎洁」。对相当一部分人来说，直接说「我爱你」有点怪怪的。</p> \n<p>因此，借第三方表达自己的情感是一个极为稳妥的方式，不管是夸赞、表白和表达关心，借别人的口说出来会更好一些。</p> \n<p>另一方面，七夕节的「孤寡」一词，巧妙暗合了如今越来越孤独的社会氛围，单身人士越来越多，人和人之间的交流越来越少，用戏谑的方式展示自己的孤独和对温暖的渴求，不失为一个「苦中作乐」的方法。</p> \n<p>正如买「线上恋人服务」的粉丝，如果她们有一个疼爱自己的男朋友，又何必把自己对爱情的美好想象寄托在虚拟服务上？如果身边有一个人时常关心自己，又何必自己买夸奖服务来夸自己？</p> \n<p>虚拟需求都是现实社会的反射，只要害羞和孤独一直存在，线上慰问服务就会好好地「活着」。</p> \n<div id=\"ifanr_profile\" style=\"border:1px solid #ccc;font-size:14px;margin:27px auto;font-family:Arial;\"> \n <div style=\"overflow:hidden\">\n  <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/author/zhuhai\" style=\"color:#000;text-decoration:none;\"></a> \n  <div style=\"text-align:left;line-height:23px;margin-left:80px\"> \n   <div style=\"padding:10px 10px 10px 0\"> \n    <div style=\"margin:0;font-size: 14px;\">\n     <strong><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/author/zhuhai\" style=\"color:#000;text-decoration:none;\">朱 海</a></strong> \n    </div> \n    <div style=\"font-size: 13px; line-height:20px;\">\n     三流方案策划者，二流出镜主持人，一流败家浪荡侠\n    </div> \n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n <div style=\"text-align:right;border-top:1px dotted #ccc;padding:2px 10px; font-size:12px;\"> \n  <div> \n   <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"mailto:zhuhai@ifanr.com\" style=\"margin-right:14px;text-decoration:none;\">邮箱</a> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p>#欢迎关注爱范儿官方微信公众号：爱范儿（微信号：ifanr），更多精彩内容第一时间为您奉上。</p>\n<p> <a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com\">爱范儿</a> | <a style=\"text-align:center;border-top:1px dotted #ccc\"> \n </div> </br>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 26 Aug 2020 10:18:20 +0000","feedId":147,"bgimg":"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14.png","linkMd5":"5de6c86a228abde7e722a6ef2cadcb28","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn28@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-03-352_5786ff71d9c836ef.webp","destWidth":1436,"destHeight":816,"sourceBytes":867502,"destBytes":867502,"author":"朱 海","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua14.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn28@2020_3/2020/08/31/17-24-03-352_5786ff71d9c836ef.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua4.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn99@2020_2/2020/08/31/17-24-28-095_68cdb77336da539d.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua5-1.png":null,"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua20.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn59@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-32-552_81bbf8b177fcaab6.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua19.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn39@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-26-038_a189488f7c20b808.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua23.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn33@2020_1/2020/08/31/17-24-32-663_64d44c7a383bafa7.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua16.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn30@2020_6/2020/08/31/17-24-25-900_27d2b901f0d9e29c.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua22.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn34@2020_5/2020/08/31/17-24-30-320_b9502f957ab6f557.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/gugua10.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn25@2020_4/2020/08/31/17-24-30-423_fc38def01abdefe8.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598894642691},{"createdTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 01:24:02","title":"3000 多元的键盘，1000 多元的鼠标垫，李楠创业发布了一批很贵的产品","link":"https://www.ifanr.com/?p=1361017&utm_source=rss&utm_medium=rss&utm_campaign=","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361068\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-1.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-1-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-1-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-1-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>作为一个外设爱好者，有数把 Filco、海盗船、赛睿以及 ROG 键盘的用户，我看到李楠从魅族离开后创立的怒喵科技发布数款外设之后，第一感觉就是「这些玩意儿真不错啊」，第二感觉则是「不过有点儿贵」。</p> \n<p>这种分裂统一的感觉在这次发布会的 B 站直播弹幕上也可以窥见一二：一拨人认为这些产品价格太高完全是资本家割韭菜；另一拨人认为价格贵不是产品的缺点是购买者自己的缺点。</p> \n<p>所以，这一次，李楠发布了什么？首先是一个名为 NOWIRE 的新品牌，寓意未来消费电子产品是无线化的。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361069\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-3.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-3-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-3-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CYBERBOARD-3-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>NOWIRE 系列新品中最先曝光的是机械键盘 CYBERBOARD，设计灵感来源于特斯拉之前发布的电动皮卡 Cybertruck，从侧面看，它的线条处理以及金属感和&nbsp;Cybertruck 神似。</p> \n<p>若说&nbsp;CYBERBOARD 和普通机械键盘最大的区别应该在于键盘前端的 LED 灯阵，这个灯阵由 200 颗 LED 灯珠组成，可以自定义出自己想要的图案，虽然不能增加生产力，但是它炫酷啊，毕竟 RGB 才是机械键盘的灵魂。</p> \n<p>其他的细节包括机身采用全铝合金 CNC 工艺，支持蓝牙 5.0 和无线充电，轴座支持热拔插。</p> \n<p>目前这个键盘的起售价为 3160 元，全球限量 1000 把。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361062\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-2.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-2-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-2-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-2-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>最后划重点说明，CYBERBOARD 不包括轴体和键帽，所以对于想买一把完整键盘的人来说，其实买到的是半成品。</p> \n<p>所以在&nbsp;CYBERBOARD 之外，李楠的怒喵科技还发布了&nbsp;CYBERSWITCH，一个自己定制的轴体。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361067\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-8.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-8.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-8-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-8-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-8-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>CYBERSWITCH 据称有段落和线性集合的手感，个人猜测可能接近樱桃茶轴那种感觉，不过既然又是 CYBER 开头的，重点自然还是赛博朋克美学。CYBERSWITCH 采用绿紫配色，半透明风格，轴体敲击声音也经过优化。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361071\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-9.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"632\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-9.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-9-360x190.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-9-768x404.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-9-1024x539.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>至于键帽，则是 NOWIRE 和 BUGER WORK 联名定制的「回到未来」主题，采用原厂高度，也就是樱桃自产键盘的那种键帽规格。材质和工艺则为 PBT 和热升华，可以避免打油和磨损现象。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361072\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-11.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"632\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-11.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-11-360x190.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-11-768x404.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-11-1024x539.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>此外还有一个 NOWIRE 和 ZOMOPLUS 合作的「时光机」金属键帽，铝合金材质，氚管自发光。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361066\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-7.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"632\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-7.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-7-360x190.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-7-768x404.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-7-1024x539.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>在组装完一把键盘之后，怒喵科技还发布了一个超大号鼠标垫，官方名为桌面超级无线充电站 CYBERMAT。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361065\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-6.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"632\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-6.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-6-360x190.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-6-768x404.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-6-1024x539.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>CYBERMAT 设计上也是受 Cybertruck 启发，外形棱角分明，金属感强烈。它最大的特点是内置了 15 个无线充电线圈，分布在三个主要充电区域，可以同时给 6 个设备进行无线充电，支持最大输入功率为 45W PD。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361064\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-5.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-5-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-5-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-5-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>不过令人意外的是，这次发布会上，怒喵科技没有发布鼠标产品，而是发布了鼠标配件：CYBERCOIN，适配于罗技 G 系列鼠标，可以让罗技 GPW 等鼠标支持 Qi 无线充电标准。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361073\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-12.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-12.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-12-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-12-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-12-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>除了桌面外设套件之外，这场发布会上还预热了一款名为 CYBERBLADE 的真无线蓝牙耳机，灵感来源自然是科幻电影《银翼杀手》，它号称有全球最低的延迟，预计 12 月底正式发布。</p> \n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361074\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-13.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-13.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-13-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-13-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-13-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /> <img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1361063\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"674\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-4.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-4-360x202.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-4-768x431.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/CB-4-1024x575.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p> \n<p>以上就是本次怒喵科技新品发布会的所有 NOWIRE 产品，除此之外，怒喵科技还投资了一些年轻品牌，比如做 T 恤的 EXT，做玩具的 AMTOYS，以及做充电设备的 SHARGE，它们也均有相关新品发布，分别是联名 T 恤、盲盒玩具以及 90W 3 口充电器。</p> \n<p>毫无疑问，在魅族旗舰主要做青年良品魅蓝手机的李楠，这一次依然把目标受众定在了青年群体上，李楠说：</p> \n<blockquote>\n <p>无线和亚文化才是科技产品的未来，怒喵科技将在三年之内跨界 12 个亚文化领域；并依托社群共创——Community Driven Creation，打造一个以科技、潮流及亚文化获得全球影响力的 HIGH-END 中国品牌。</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>不过很明显，这些产品在售价上就区隔开了普通大众：没有轴体和键帽的键帽售价 3160 元，超大号鼠标垫&nbsp;CYBERMAT 售价 1380 元，90 颗&nbsp;CYBERSWITCH 轴体售价 720 元，CYBER 系列桌面大礼包一共 6200 元… 也就是说，伴随着限量、联名、盲盒、组装等玩法的出现，这些产品就有了更多的附加价值，就像二级市场的潮鞋那样。</p> \n<p>就在这篇文章还没写完的时候，那个贵到不行的 6200 套装和 3160 键盘，也都宣告售罄。</p> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<div id=\"ifanr_profile\" style=\"border:1px solid #ccc;font-size:14px;margin:27px auto;font-family:Arial;\"> \n <div style=\"overflow:hidden\">\n  <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/author/owen\" style=\"color:#000;text-decoration:none;\"></a> \n  <div style=\"text-align:left;line-height:23px;margin-left:80px\"> \n   <div style=\"padding:10px 10px 10px 0\"> \n    <div style=\"margin:0;font-size: 14px;\">\n     <strong><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/author/owen\" style=\"color:#000;text-decoration:none;\">刘学文</a></strong> \n    </div> \n    <div style=\"font-size: 13px; line-height:20px;\">\n     在命运的塑料大棚里，每棵被喷了过多农药的白菜心中，都曾经有一个成为无公害有机蔬菜的梦想。\n    </div> \n   </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n <div style=\"text-align:right;border-top:1px dotted
